<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=FreeWin_Invitational/Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>September 28th - October 5th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>One group of six teams</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top four teams</span> proceed to the Playoffs</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom two teams</span> are eliminated</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b> - <i>October 6th - October 9th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Double-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadcast_Talent">Broadcast Talent</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=FreeWin_Invitational/Europe&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Broadcast Talent">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Caster:</b>
